SELECT [i].[Id], [i].[Description], [i].[Type], [i].[Status], [i].[Location_Latitude] AS [Latitude], [i].[Location_Longitude] AS [Longitude], [i].[ImagePath] AS [BeforeImagePath], [i].[ResolvedImagePath] AS [AfterImagePath], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [u].[Name]
    FROM [IssueAssignments] AS [i0]
    INNER JOIN [Workers] AS [w] ON [i0].[WorkerId] = [w].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [w].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
    WHERE [i].[Id] = [i0].[IssueId]) AS [AssignedWorkerName], COALESCE((
    SELECT TOP(1) [i1].[Salary]
    FROM [IssueAssignments] AS [i1]
    WHERE [i].[Id] = [i1].[IssueId]), 0.0) AS [Salary], COALESCE((
    SELECT TOP(1) [i2].[Deadline]
    FROM [IssueAssignments] AS [i2]
    WHERE [i].[Id] = [i2].[IssueId]), '0001-01-01T00:00:00.0000000') AS [Deadline], [i].[RejectionReason]
FROM [Issues] AS [i]
ORDER BY [i].[CreatedAt] DESC
